It's like Cheers.  All the staff knows my name :-)  Always a familiar face there.  Lots of locals.  A great Leucadia hangout.  A ton of taps.  No food is served, but you can bring food in from neighboring restaurants.  Dogs welcome.  A very cool casual place.  Love it!<//Text>

<Review>Came here for the first time with my wife and a friend and had a blast! There was such a wide range of great sounding beers that the three of us decided to each get a flight of four and share them amongst us.

The service was great and the staff was very helpful when we were picking out our 12 selections.

I liked almost all the beers we tried but they've got something special with their 'Orange Guava IPA'.

This place was easy and casual and I would suggest stopping by for a pint. They seem to have something for everyone.<//Review>< response>

While I'm not an employee, I am an online host for Dentsply Sirona, the American dental equipment maker and leading dental consumables producer that markets its products in over 120 countries. Knowing a company with a background as solid and reputable as they are, I was certain a dentist who believed in their products would be a dentist I could believe in. Here's my bottom line: Being new members of the Encinitas community, my wife and I are big supporters of "local" and do what we can to improve the business of "the little guy." < Review>
This church is so peaceful Monday - Friday. I come here to be alone and pray, sometimes bringing relatives or friends. I cannot bring words to the peace it brings you, in the middle of a bustling city and it quiets your mind, even for a brief moment. Stop at the small office beyond the gate, knock on the gated black screen door and ask for a candle or two, they are $3 each and come with a match so you may take it i side the church and light it before praying. There is a small cave like vestibule in one front corner and many candles and prayers can be found there.</Review>
